SELECT PM.ItemCode, PM.Category, PM.Description, TP.UOM,  
PM.ItemType,  
PM.Brand, PM.Classifications, PM.DisplayOrder, round(TP.PRICECASES,2), 
TP.DISCOUNT, BN.BrandName,R.Quantity, R.UOM,BN.BrandImage, 
PM.CustomerGroupCodes,PM.Classifications,PM.Description3, 
G.Priority as priority, 'MSL' as classification, PM.Description1, PM.UnitBarCode, TCI.CustomerItemCode, PM.DefinUOM,PM.VATCD   
 FROM tblProducts PM INNER JOIN tblPricing TP ON PM.DisplayOrder != 'P92' AND TP.ITEMCODE = PM.ItemCode AND TP.CUSTOMERPRICINGKEY = '12'  AND DATE('now') between DATE(TP.STARTDATE) and DATE(TP.ENDDATE)  
INNER JOIN tblBrand BN ON BN.BrandId = PM.Brand  
INNER JOIN tblSellingSKU S ON S.ItemCode = PM.ItemCode AND S.GroupType = 'Channel' AND S.GroupCode ='2'  
INNER JOIN tblGroupSellingSKUClassification  G ON G.SellingSKUId  = S.SellingSKUId AND G.SellingSKUClassificationId ='1'  
LEFT OUTER JOIN tblRecommendedOrder R ON R.ItemCode = S.ItemCode AND R.ClientCode = 'A1092-001' AND Date like '2023-02-21%'  
LEFT OUTER JOIN tblCustomerSpecificItem TCI ON TCI.ItemCode = TP.ItemCode AND TCI.CustomerCode = 'A1092'  
 WHERE PM.CategoryLevel5='Y' GROUP BY PM.ItemCode  
UNION

TP.DISCOUNT, BN.BrandName,R.Quantity, R.UOM,BN.BrandImage, 
PM.CustomerGroupCodes,PM.Classifications,PM.Description3, 
G.Priority as priority, 'Focus' as classification, PM.Description1, PM.UnitBarCode, TCI.CustomerItemCode, PM.DefinUOM,PM.VATCD  
FROM tblProducts PM INNER JOIN tblPricing TP ON PM.DisplayOrder != 'P92' AND TP.ITEMCODE = PM.ItemCode AND length(trim(TP.CUSTOMERPRICINGKEY)) = 0  AND DATE('now') between DATE(TP.STARTDATE) and DATE(TP.ENDDATE)  
INNER JOIN tblBrand BN ON BN.BrandId = PM.Brand  
INNER JOIN tblSellingSKU S ON S.ItemCode = PM.ItemCode AND S.GroupType = 'Channel' AND S.GroupCode ='2'  
INNER JOIN tblGroupSellingSKUClassification  G ON G.SellingSKUId  = S.SellingSKUId AND G.SellingSKUClassificationId ='2'  
LEFT OUTER JOIN tblRecommendedOrder R ON R.ItemCode = S.ItemCode AND R.ClientCode = 'A837-001' AND Date like '2023-02-24%'  
LEFT OUTER JOIN tblCustomerSpecificItem TCI ON TCI.ItemCode = TP.ItemCode AND TCI.CustomerCode = 'A837'  
WHERE PM.ItemCode NOT IN (SELECT ItemCode FROM tblPricing R WHERE R.CUSTOMERPRICINGKEY = '12' AND R.IsExpired = 'False' COLLATE NOCASE)  AND PM.CategoryLevel5='Y' GROUP BY PM.ItemCode  Union SELECT PM.ItemCode, PM.Category, PM.Description, TP.UOM, 
PM.ItemType, PM.Brand, PM.Classifications, PM.DisplayOrder,  
round(TP.PRICECASES,2),TP.DISCOUNT, BN.BrandName,R.Quantity,  
R.UOM,BN.BrandImage,PM.CustomerGroupCodes,PM.Classifications, 
PM.Description3 ,1000000 as priority, 'ALL' as classification,  PM.Description1, PM.UnitBarCode, TCI.CustomerItemCode, PM.DefinUOM,PM.VATCD   
FROM tblProducts PM INNER JOIN tblPricing TP ON PM.DisplayOrder != 'P92' AND TP.ITEMCODE = PM.ItemCode AND TP.CUSTOMERPRICINGKEY = '12' AND DATE('now') between DATE(TP.STARTDATE) and DATE(TP.ENDDATE)  
INNER JOIN tblBrand BN ON BN.BrandId = PM.Brand  
INNER JOIN tblSellingSKU S ON S.ItemCode = PM.ItemCode AND S.GroupType = 'Channel' AND S.GroupCode ='2' 
LEFT OUTER JOIN tblRecommendedOrder R ON R.ItemCode = TP.ItemCode AND R.ClientCode = 'A837-001' AND Date like '2023-02-24%'  
LEFT OUTER JOIN tblCustomerSpecificItem TCI ON TCI.ItemCode = TP.ItemCode AND TCI.CustomerCode = 'A837'  
 WHERE PM.CategoryLevel5='Y' GROUP BY PM.ItemCode

TP.DISCOUNT, BN.BrandName,R.Quantity, R.UOM,BN.BrandImage, 
PM.CustomerGroupCodes,PM.Classifications,PM.Description3, 
1000000 as priority,  'ALL' as classification,  
PM.Description1, PM.UnitBarCode, TCI.CustomerItemCode, PM.DefinUOM,PM.VATCD   
FROM tblProducts PM INNER JOIN tblPricing TP ON PM.DisplayOrder != 'P92' AND TP.ITEMCODE = PM.ItemCode AND length(trim(TP.CUSTOMERPRICINGKEY)) = 0  AND DATE('now') between DATE(TP.STARTDATE) and DATE(TP.ENDDATE)  
INNER JOIN tblBrand BN ON BN.BrandId = PM.Brand  
INNER JOIN tblSellingSKU S ON S.ItemCode = PM.ItemCode AND S.GroupType = 'Channel' AND S.GroupCode ='2'  
LEFT OUTER JOIN tblRecommendedOrder R ON R.ItemCode = TP.ItemCode AND R.ClientCode = 'J114-001' AND Date like '2023-03-10%'  
LEFT OUTER JOIN tblCustomerSpecificItem TCI ON TCI.ItemCode = TP.ItemCode AND TCI.CustomerCode = 'J114'  
WHERE PM.ItemCode NOT IN (SELECT ItemCode FROM tblPricing R WHERE R.CUSTOMERPRICINGKEY = '12' AND R.IsExpired = 'False' COLLATE NOCASE) AND PM.CategoryLevel5='Y'  
GROUP BY PM.ItemCode  Union SELECT PM.ItemCode, PM.Category, PM.Description, TP.UOM, 
PM.ItemType, PM.Brand, PM.Classifications, PM.DisplayOrder,  
round(TP.PRICECASES,2),TP.DISCOUNT, BN.BrandName,R.Quantity,  
R.UOM,BN.BrandImage,PM.CustomerGroupCodes,PM.Classifications, 
PM.Description3 ,1000000 as priority, 'ALL' as classification,  PM.Description1, PM.UnitBarCode, TCI.CustomerItemCode, PM.DefinUOM,PM.VATCD   
FROM tblProducts PM INNER JOIN tblPricing TP ON PM.DisplayOrder != 'P92' AND TP.ITEMCODE = PM.ItemCode AND TP.CUSTOMERPRICINGKEY = '12' AND DATE('now') between DATE(TP.STARTDATE) and DATE(TP.ENDDATE)  
INNER JOIN tblBrand BN ON BN.BrandId = PM.Brand  
INNER JOIN tblSellingSKU S ON S.ItemCode = PM.ItemCode AND S.GroupType = 'Channel' AND S.GroupCode ='2' 
LEFT OUTER JOIN tblRecommendedOrder R ON R.ItemCode = TP.ItemCode AND R.ClientCode = 'J114-001' AND Date like '2023-03-10%'  
LEFT OUTER JOIN tblCustomerSpecificItem TCI ON TCI.ItemCode = TP.ItemCode AND TCI.CustomerCode = 'J114'  
 WHERE PM.CategoryLevel5='Y' GROUP BY PM.ItemCode   
UNION
